        let state = url.searchParams.get("state")

        let URLdomain = ".clarin.com"

    function cerrar2() {
        document.getElementById("b-main-top").style.display='none';
    }
    
    myID = document.getElementById("b-main-top");
    
    var myScrollFunc = function () {
        var y = window.scrollY;
        if (y >= 100) {
            myID.className = "b-visible"
        } else {
            myID.className = "b-hidden"
        }
    };
    
    window.addEventListener("scroll", myScrollFunc);
</script>

    //         let refClassNodemand = "moduleClass_CLAClarinContentBMO " + refClass

    $(document).on('domReady.OnDemand', function(event){
        if ( "IntersectionObserver" in window && "IntersectionObserverEntry" in window ) {
            LazyImages()
        }
    });

    var el = $(".on-demand").eq(0);

    // console.log("ELEMENTOS ", $(".on-demand"))

    var acum = 1;

    var updateOnDemand = function(e) {
        e.html('<div class="demand-loading"><i class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin"></i></div>');
       
        $(window).unbind("scroll.OnDemand");

        $.get(e.data("src"), function(_response) {
            response = BBT.fixJson(_response);
            if (response.error == 0) {
                // e.html(response.data);
                $(response.data).insertAfter(e);
				optaLoader.findWidget();

                console.log("ONDEMAND", e.attr("id"), $(".on-demand").length, acum)
                if ( acum < $(".on-demand").length ) {
                    el = $(".on-demand").eq(acum++);
                    updateBody();
                }
               
                if(typeof(jQuery)=='undefined'){
                	onDemandEvent = document.createEvent('Event');
	                onDemandEvent.initEvent('domReady.OnDemand', false, false, undefined);
	                document.dispatchEvent(onDemandEvent);
                }else{
                	$(document).triggerHandler('domReady.OnDemand');
                }
                sendRequestToXML();
            }
        }).fail(function() {
            $(".demand-loading").remove();
        });
    }

    var isiPad = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;

    function checkScroll(e) {
        var modificacionLimiteScroll = 350;

        if (isiPad && ($(window).height()>=$(window).width())) {
            modificacionLimiteScroll = 25;
        };
        
        if ( ( $(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height() + 5  ) >= ((e.parent().offset().top)) - modificacionLimiteScroll ) {
            console.log(e.parent().offset(), acum)
            console.log('updateOnDemand', $(window).scrollTop(), $(window).height(),  e.parent().offset().top)
            // test = $(".on-demand").eq(acum)
            // console.log(test)
            // console.log('TEMPLATE', test.outerHeight(true));
            updateOnDemand(e); 
        }
    }

    function updateBody () {
        if ($(window).height() >= $("body").height() ) {
            
            updateOnDemand(el);

        } else {
            $(window).bind("scroll.OnDemand", function(){
                checkScroll(el);
            })
        }
    }

	if ( typeof el.html() != "undefined" ){
	    updateBody();
	}
</script>
<script type="application/javascript">

    function GDPRInit() {

        var scriptJS = document.createElement('script');

        if(scriptJS.readyState) {
            scriptJS.onreadystatechange = function() {
                if ( scriptJS.readyState === "loaded" || scriptJS.readyState === "complete" ) {
                    scriptJS.onreadystatechange = null;
                    GDPRStart()
                }
            };
        } else{//others
                scriptJS.onload = function() {
                GDPRStart()
                }
            }
    scriptJS.src = "/commons/js/GDPRCookiePolicy.js";
    document.documentElement.appendChild(scriptJS);

    }

    _clarin = {};
    _clarin.sw = {
        serviceWorker: null
    };

    function SWInit() {
        var _filereC = document.createElement("link")
        _filereC.setAttribute("rel", "stylesheet")
        _filereC.setAttribute("type", "text/css")
        _filereC.setAttribute("href", "/commons/sw/sw-app.css")
        document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(_filereC);

        var _scripts = [
            "/commons/sw/firebaseconf.js",
            "/commons/sw/sw-app.js",
            "/commons/sw/init.js?v=0.3"];

        for(i=0;i<3;i++) {
            var _scriptJS = document.createElement('script');
            _scriptJS.src = _scripts[i];
            document.documentElement.appendChild(_scriptJS);
        }
    }

    $(document).on('wa.ready', function() {
        var appVersion = navigator.appVersion;
        var iOS = (/iphone|ipad|ipod/gi).test(appVersion);

        if(!iOS) SWInit();
    });

	var loc = this.getValueFromCookie("location")
	var region = this.getValueFromCookie("region")

	if(loc == "" || region == ""){
		$.ajax({
		    type: 'GET',
		    url: 'https://api-editoriales.clarin.com/0778a0d2d20704cc978389c74565352e/042505ecee3f71651eced5be4c90905e',
		    success: function(respuesta) {

		    	if(typeof(respuesta.item.data) != "undefined" && respuesta.item.data != null){
		    		
		    	document.cookie = "location="+respuesta.item.data;
					document.cookie = "region="+respuesta.item.details.region;

		        if(respuesta.item.details.region == "Europe"){
					  	GDPRInit();
					  }
          }
		    },
		});

	}else{

		if(region == "Europe"){
			GDPRInit();
		}
	}

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var refreshChecker = {
            init : function () {
                var data =  this.getValueFromCookie("autorefresh").split("|");
                if ( data[0] == '' || data[0] != window.location.pathname) {
                    this.setValueToCookie("autorefresh",window.location.pathname + "|0");
                } else if (data[0] == window.location.pathname  &&  data[1] == "0" ) {
                    this.setValueToCookie("autorefresh", window.location.pathname + "|1");
                }
            },
            getValueFromCookie :function (cookieName)
            {
                var reg = cookieName + '\\=([^\\;]+)';
                var matches = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(reg));
                return matches != null && matches.length > 1 ? matches[1] : '';
            },
            setValueToCookie: function (cookieName, value) {
                document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + value + ";path=/;";
            },

            delete_cookie: function (name) {
                document.cookie = name + '=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;path=/;';
            },
            isAutorefresh: function () {
                var data = this.getValueFromCookie("autorefresh").split("|");
                return typeof data[1] != 'undefined' ? data[1] : "0";
            },
    }
    refreshChecker.init();
</script>
